		<script type="text/javascript">
const urlInfo = {
	'staticUrl': "https://img10.naventcdn.com/ficha/HF-RPFICv5.251.1-RC2/",
}
let createNameRelease = (urlInfo) => {
const completeURL = urlInfo.staticUrl
const indexOfH = completeURL.indexOf("H")
const indexOfR = completeURL.indexOf("R")
let releaseString = ''
if (indexOfH !== -1) {
	releaseString = completeURL.substring(indexOfH)
} else {
	releaseString = completeURL.substring(indexOfR)
}
const indexOfV = releaseString.indexOf("v")
const releaseInfo = {
	name: releaseString.substring(0, indexOfV),
	id: releaseString.substring(indexOfV).replace('/', '')
}
return releaseInfo
}
const release = createNameRelease(urlInfo)
</script>
